                      <div data-reactid="297">
                       My home is located in a calm and safe neighborhood of Costa Mesa, a short 5 minute drive to Newport Beach. The house is a cozy 3 bedroom rancho built in the early 50's &amp; nestled between 2 large front and back yards (no pets). You will share the house with me alone. Parking is always available right in front of home!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="298">
                       Your bedroom is 14 x 12 with plenty of room for luggage. * Featherbed Queen mattress which is highly comfortable, I am told. * Stonewashed cotton linen sheets, down duvet &amp; pillows (4) * Fresh linens and towels provided. * Walk in closet with wood hangers. * Hard wood throughout. * Black out blinds * Door lock. * Shared bath (very clean). All my belongings are in drawers so the space is yours. Hair dryer and bathroom essentials available. * No smoking in the house but you have a backyard where you can light up. * Parking is free and ALWAYS available right in front of the house. No street sweeping ever. * Light breakfast is provided. Please check house manual for details. Let me know if you have any questions or requests before you travel. I'll try &amp; make your stay as pleasant as possible.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="299">
                       The neighborhood is safe and quiet. I have included my favorite spots (restaurants, to shopping, to bars) in the guidebook. Most of the businesses are located on 17th street on the south side of Newport Boulevard. There are a few spots near us that I recommend. Feel free to ask me for anything I have not listed. Bike path If you have time to explore, I recommend renting a bike (see guidebook for details) and/ or SUP (Stand Up Paddle) / kayak. You can rent one for the day and cruise around the harbor. It's a ton of fun! The bike path which is 2 minutes East from my place. The Santa Ana river path takes you up to 70 miles inland or you can choose the Huntington Beach / Newport trail which is 13 miles long, right on the beach. For performing arts, check out our Segerstrom Center / Pacific Symphony. They always have something worth seeing and sell tickets for all budgets.

                      <div data-reactid="1165">
                       This historic landmark home, built in 1907, is a 7 bedroom Craftsman house with a large corner yard shaded by an enormous sycamore tree. From the porch, the sun and moon rise through the branches. Watching them from the rocking chairs you might think yourself in Savannah were it not for the soothing sound of the world class waves just down the street. The room is cozy with two windows for amazing light and refreshing ocean air. There is a comfy 4 post queen bed with 100% Egyptian cotton linens as well as a small antique writing desk and a large closet.

There are several world class surf spots in walking distance, including the world famous Huntington Beach Pier.

                       Huntington Harbor Waterfront Home Let this exquisite waterfront Tuscan estate be the getaway destination of your dreams. Prestigious location puts you close to all So. The bedroom suite on the main floor has a queen size bed, opulent bath, mini kitchen and flat screen. Laundry on both floors. Another bedroom upstairs with a king size bed flat screen, opens to full balcony for channel view. Another bedroom is used for an office/workout room, but is equipped with a comfortable queen sized Murphy bed. All upstairs bedrooms have views and open to the expansive wrap around deck.
